RETRIEVAL_BASIC
---------------
R01. Who are the ladies that had relationship with Jose Rizal?
R02. Who killed Ferdinand Magellan?
R03. Did Lapu-Lapu kill Magellan?
R04. Who is the first Philippine president?
R05. What did the Treaty of Paris of 1898 say about the Philippines?
R06. What hardships did Filipinos experience during the Japanese occupation?

DIRECT
------
D01. Who was Apolinario Mabini and what role did he serve in the First Philippine Republic?
D02. Sino si Andres Bonifacio?

KEYWORD_HEAVY
-------------
K01. Who founded the Katipunan or KKK on July 7, 1892, and what was its purpose against Spain?
K02. Who were the Gomburza priests executed by garrote after the 1872 Cavite Mutiny, and how were they connected to secularization, the friars, Rizal, and El filibusterismo?

PARAPHRASED
-----------
P01. Which secret group tried to free Filipinos from Spanish rule through armed revolution before it was discovered in 1896?
P02. Which leader was called the Brains of the Revolution because of his role as adviser to the revolutionary government?

TAGALOG_ENGLISH_DOCS
--------------------
T01. Kailan ipinagdiriwang ang Araw ng Kalayaan ng Pilipinas at anong pangyayari ang ginugunita nito?
T02. Ano ang nangyari sa Pilipinas noong World War II nang sakupin ito ng Japan?

NEGATIVE_UNANSWERABLE
---------------------
N01. What was Andres Bonifacio's official passport number during the Philippine Revolution?
N02. Ano ang eksaktong Wi-Fi password na ginamit ng Katipunan sa kanilang mga pagpupulong?

CROSS_DOC
---------
X01. How did the Treaty of Paris connect the Spanish-American War to the Philippine-American War?
X02. How is José Rizal’s La Liga Filipina related to the founding of the Katipunan?

FALSE_PREMISE
-------------
F01. Why did Jose Rizal become the Supremo of the Katipunan?
F02. Bakit si Apolinario Mabini ang nagdeklara ng kalayaan ng Pilipinas noong June 12, 1898?

SIMILAR_TOPIC
-------------
S01. Compare the Spanish-American War vs. the Philippine-American War. Do not interchange the cause and result of the two wars.
S02. What is the difference between the Philippine Revolution and the Katipunan? Is one an organization and the other a war/revolution?
